MSGS['MessageFormatter']={
paramRegExpArray:[],
getParamRegExp:function(p){
var r=this.paramRegExpArray[p];
if(!r){
r=new RegExp('\\{' + p + '\\}', 'g');
this.paramRegExpArray[p]=r;
}
return r;
},
format:function(pattern){
var r=pattern,
p=0,
i;
if(r&&r.replace){
for(i=1;i<arguments.length;i++){
r=r.replace(this.getParamRegExp(p++),arguments[i]);
}
}
return r;
}
};
MSGS['get']=function(k){
if(arguments.length>1){
var d=new Array(arguments.length),
i,
f=this.MessageFormatter;
for(i=1;i<arguments.length;i++){
d[i]=arguments[i];
}
d[0]=this[k];
return f.format.apply(f,d);
}else{
return this[k];
}
};
function MessageFormatter(){}
MessageFormatter.prototype.format=function(){
var f=MSGS.MessageFormatter;
return f.format.apply(f,arguments);
};

        function create_page_header_model() {
            function text(id) {
                var el = document.getElementById(id);
                return (el && (el.innerText || el.textContent)) || '';
            }
            if (!window.pageHeaderJsonData) {
                return null;
            }

            };
        }

                    function renderPageHeaderFunc(containerID) {
                        if (window.pageHeaderJsonData && typeof SFResponsiveHeader != 'undefined') {
                            pageHeaderComp = new SFResponsiveHeader(create_page_header_model());
                            pageHeaderComp.render(containerID || 'renderTopNavFixedWidthV12');
                        }
                    }
                    if (window.SFDOMEvent) {
                        SFDOMEvent.ready({
                            priority: 'HIGH',
                            callback: renderPageHeaderFunc
                        });
                    } else if (window.jQuery) {
                        jQuery(jQuery.proxy(renderPageHeaderFunc, null, null));
                    }



                window.isV2Enabled = true;
   
            function pageOnLoad() {
                window.selectedUserID = "100106061";
                window.companyId = "ICRCTEST1";
                window.workflowRequestId = Util.escapeHTML(juic.$("RequestId").value);
                window.workflowRequestStepId = Util.escapeHTML(juic.$("StepId").value);
                window.isFromWorkflowPage = true;
                window.workflowApproval = new ECTWorkflowApprovalController();
                window.ECTLoadingMgr.showLoading();
                window.workflowApproval.render("workflowApprovalBody");
                window.workflowApproval.getDataByWFRequestId();
                <!-- always show help icons if defined for field in ectHelpLinkMap.js -->
                window.isHelpAvailable = true;
                window.isDisableContentDensity = false;
                /*ECT-59396,59397,59398 : GACE search widget adoption 
                 *Need to check whether GA/CE is enabled, from companySettings to enbale new search widget for delegate workflow page 
                 */ 
            ECTSearchAdoptionUtils.setGACEEnabled(false,false,true);
            
            /**
            * ECT-111423 : Force new search 
            */
            ECTSearchAdoptionUtils.setForceNewSearch(true);
            
            }

            jQuery(document).ready(pageOnLoad);



//--></script><!-- MYFACES JAVASCRIPT -->
